Under the new scoring system, each PSLE subject will be scored using 8 Achievement Levels (ALs), with AL 1 being the best. <script type="text/javascript">
	 jQuery(".InterestedProgramme").click(function(){
	let first_cus = ""
	
var cboxes = document.getElementsByName('InterestedProgramme[]');
    var len = cboxes.length;
    for (var i=0; i<len; i++) {
if(cboxes[i].checked){
	if(first_cus == ""){
		first_cus = cboxes[i].value
	}else{
		first_cus = first_cus.concat(" " +cboxes[i].value)
	}
	
}
    }

jQuery("#ip_hidden").val(first_cus);
  });
</script>
